## Diagram 3

```mermaid
graph TB
    subgraph ClusterRole[Descheduler ClusterRole]
        subgraph EventsAPI[events.k8s.io]
            Events1[events]
            EventsVerbs1[create, update]
            Events1 --> EventsVerbs1
        end
        subgraph CoreAPI[Core API Group]
            Nodes1[nodes]
            NodesVerbs1[get, watch, list]
            Nodes1 --> NodesVerbs1
            Namespaces1[namespaces]
            NamespacesVerbs1[get, watch, list]
            Namespaces1 --> NamespacesVerbs1
            Pods1[pods]
            PodsVerbs1[get, watch, list, delete]
            Pods1 --> PodsVerbs1
            PodEviction1[pods/eviction]
            PodEvictionVerbs1[create]
            PodEviction1 --> PodEvictionVerbs1
        end
        subgraph SchedulingAPI[scheduling.k8s.io]
            Priority1[priorityclasses]
            PriorityVerbs1[get, watch, list]
            Priority1 --> PriorityVerbs1
        end
        subgraph CoordinationAPI[coordination.k8s.io]
            Leases1[leases]
            LeasesVerbs1[create, update, get, patch, delete]
            Leases1 --> LeasesVerbs1
        end
    end
```

## Diagram 4

```mermaid
classDiagram
    class ClusterRole {
        +String name
        +Map labels
        +List rules
    }
    class Rule {
        +List apiGroups
        +List resources
        +List verbs
        +List resourceNames
    }
    class EventsRule {
        apiGroups: events.k8s.io
        resources: events
        verbs: create, update
    }
    class NodesRule {
        apiGroups: core
        resources: nodes
        verbs: get, watch, list
    }
    class NamespacesRule {
        apiGroups: core
        resources: namespaces
        verbs: get, watch, list
    }
    class PodsRule {
        apiGroups: core
        resources: pods
        verbs: get, watch, list, delete
    }
    class PodEvictionRule {
        apiGroups: core
        resources: pods/eviction
        verbs: create
    }
    class PriorityClassesRule {
        apiGroups: scheduling.k8s.io
        resources: priorityclasses
        verbs: get, watch, list
    }
    class LeasesRule {
        apiGroups: coordination.k8s.io
        resources: leases
        verbs: create, update, get, patch, delete
    }
    ClusterRole "1" --> "*" Rule
    Rule <|-- EventsRule
    Rule <|-- NodesRule
    Rule <|-- NamespacesRule
    Rule <|-- PodsRule
    Rule <|-- PodEvictionRule
    Rule <|-- PriorityClassesRule
    Rule <|-- LeasesRule
```

## Diagram 5

```mermaid
stateDiagram-v2
    [*] --> CheckRBACCreate
    CheckRBACCreate --> DefineClusterRole: rbac.create = true
    CheckRBACCreate --> [*]: rbac.create = false
    DefineClusterRole --> AddCorePermissions
    AddCorePermissions --> AddEventPermissions
    AddEventPermissions --> AddSchedulingPermissions
    AddSchedulingPermissions --> CheckLeaderElection
    CheckLeaderElection --> AddLeaderElectionPermissions: leaderElection.enabled = true
    CheckLeaderElection --> Completed: leaderElection.enabled = false
    AddLeaderElectionPermissions --> Completed
    Completed --> [*]
```
